So, trying to be somewhat cost conscientious I went with the coastal scents palette...also because of the many youtube positive reviews it got.<br /><br />The palette is quite large, and so many colors to mix, match, and play around with. I use the lighter colors as a highlighter above my cheeks, and below my brow. I use the two middle colors (top and bottom) as they are closest to my skin color (depending on the area of application). I use the darker colors for contouring or as an eye shadow base. So, I know I'll use every color at some point.<br /><br />The consistency is a dry/dense cream. It is easy to apply with patting motion (no swiping). They are buildable too, I tried mixing before applying - it just gets the colors muddy - so will be mixing another way.<br /><br />I did a few test applications on my various problem areas - dark sunspots (main concern), broken capillaries on my nose, spider veins on my cheeks, blemishes from acne, dark area under my eyes.<br /><br />Each test was with a clean face, toned, moisturized, and primer applied. The first test was just the concealer by itself - patted on with my ring finger. It did okay, but I had to apply a few layers for it to really cover my problem areas...and started getting cakey under the eyes. Plus, it never completely hid my sunspots, unless I had a thick layer (which I don't want to do - bad look). The second test was with the Graftobian Color Correctors applied first in a thin layer over my problem areas. Waited a minute to let the correctors adjust and settle, then applied this concealer (by patting again with my ring finger). Most of my problem areas were covered. Even the sun spot was covered for a little bit. Both times I set lightly with powder - pressing it in to the areas. But, my dilemma was evident! I had not applied foundation! So, my next test was the same as above but with foundation first - liquid applied with a damp beauty blender. Slightly better results. My last test - my favorite, is to apply thin layers of the color corrector, then concealer, then Airbrush my foundation. I prefer this method instead of several layers of just airbrushing...it would get too dry and think in some places. But, by these multiple layers, I don't have to use a lot of any one product, and they layer quite well together. AND I can use some of the darker concealer to do my contouring so it's a more &#34;blended&#34; look with my airbrush. I'm happy with my purchase.

The coverage is really, really good. I would say that if, on a scale of 1 to 10, where Mac Full Coverage cream foundation is a 10, this Coastal Scents concealer rates around an 8 in the coverage department. Seriously. And the colors - these do not seam to oxidize at all (how do they do that?) - so you don't have to wait a few minutes to see what you are going to look like for real. (No one knows the secret of fear of women where we put on our makeup and look good-to-go, then you arrive at your destination only to find out that you are orange or something because your makeup oxidized on your way to work or to the event, and now there is nothing you can do about it! Right?) I wish this company sold some foundations here on Amazon, because I would be the first to buy. Also something I've noticed, it's not \\"sticky\\" for your next layer (blush, for instance). Most cream concealers I've ever used will grab onto blush or other powders and make them more vibrant - which would be great if you put concealer under the entire area you were applying the powder - but of course, one little dot where you concealed some flaw being really dark pink is not cute. And lastly, on bare skin, this looks like skin...it's a little greasy at first, but it fills in pores and goes into little lines and blends really well. I once used it in a hurry and in bad lighting, when I had no makeup on and someone showed up unexpectedly (under eyes, a pimple, around my nose in about 2 minutes) - and I was surprised how decent it looked - it melted into my bare skin right away and was totally undetectable. I would consider wearing nothing but this concealer in the summer with a setting spray, for that 'I swear, I'm not wearing any makeup, wink wink' look.
